## 🧩 Components

### 📦 Icon wrapper

**Variants:**

| Variant | Size |
|---|---|
| `Size=2xs (12)` | 2xs (12) |
| `Size=xs (16)` | xs (16) |
| `Size=sm (20)` | sm (20) |
| `Size=md (24)` | md (24) |
| `Size=lg (32)` | lg (32) |
| `Size=xlg (40)` | xlg (40) |

#### Variant Token Differences

| Variant | Fill | Border Radius | Effects |
|---|---|---|---|
| `Size=2xs (12)` | - | - | - |
| `Size=xs (16)` | - | - | - |
| `Size=sm (20)` | - | - | - |
| `Size=md (24)` | - | - | - |
| `Size=lg (32)` | - | - | - |
| `Size=xlg (40)` | - | - | - |

|---|---|---|

| `Store=One Store, Style=Black` | One Store | Black |
| `Store=F-Droid, Style=Black` | F-Droid | Black |
| `Store=Google Play, Style=Outline` | Google Play | Outline |
| `Store=App Store, Style=Outline` | App Store | Outline |
| `Store=Microsoft, Style=Outline` | Microsoft | Outline |
| `Store=Galaxy Store, Style=Outline` | Galaxy Store | Outline |

| `Store=AppGallery, Style=Outline` | AppGallery | Outline |

| `Store=One Store, Style=Outline` | One Store | Outline |
| `Store=F-Droid, Style=Outline` | F-Droid | Outline |

**Border Radius:** 5px

| Variant | Fill | Border Radius | Effects |
|---|---|---|---|
| `Store=Google Play, Style=Black` | #000000 | 5px | - |
| `Store=App Store, Style=Black` | #0C0D10 | 7px | - |
| `Store=Microsoft, Style=Black` | #000000 | - | - |
| `Store=Galaxy Store, Style=Black` | #231F20 | 7.25px | - |
| `Store=Amazon Appstore, Style=Black` | #100F0D | 5px | - |
| `Store=AppGallery, Style=Black` | #100F0D | 6.75px | - |
| `Store=Chromebook, Style=Black` | #000000 | 6px | - |
| `Store=One Store, Style=Black` | #000000 | 4.75px | - |
| `Store=F-Droid, Style=Black` | #000000 | 5px | - |
| `Store=Google Play, Style=Outline` | #FFFFFF | 5px | - |
| `Store=App Store, Style=Outline` | #FFFFFF | 7px | - |
| `Store=Microsoft, Style=Outline` | #FFFFFF | - | - |
| `Store=Galaxy Store, Style=Outline` | #FFFFFF | 7.25px | - |

## 🤖 Usage Guide (for AI Coding Tools)

When building UI with this design system:

1. **Always use token values** – never hardcode raw hex or px values
2. **Match component variants exactly** – use the variant names from the tables above
3. **Respect auto-layout rules** – components have defined padding, gap, and direction
4. **Apply bound tokens** – use the token names listed in 'Bound Tokens' for each component

### Example Prompt Template

```
Using the design system spec above, build a [COMPONENT NAME] component in React.
- Use variant: [VARIANT NAME]
- Apply fill token: [TOKEN NAME]
- Use typography: [FONT SIZE / WEIGHT from spec]
- Border radius: [VALUE from spec]
- Layout: [direction / gap / padding from spec]
```
